A communication from Zhenjiang stated that the Shanghai Local Association, concerned about the excessively low rice prices in various regions, causing hardship for farmers and merchants, specifically sent letters to enthusiastic leaders of organizations in Jiangsu Province that produce a large amount of rice, appointing representatives to gather in Wuxi on the 17th and 18th of this month. A joint meeting was held at the County Chamber of Commerce, attended by twenty-four leaders and commercial representatives from various places, including Suzhou, Changzhou, Wuxi, and Yu, and invited Director He of the Industry Department and County Magistrate Chen of Wuxi to attend. The main purpose of this meeting was to unite officials and the people to first organize the Jiangsu Province People's Food Regulation Association. The membership should include representatives from the Civil Affairs, Finance, and Industry Departments, the banking sector, chambers of commerce from rice-producing areas, the financial sector, farmers' banks, and other reputable and impartial individuals. In addition to the twenty-four representatives from various places who attended the meeting and acted as initiators, Wang Xiaolai from Shanghai, Yang Hanxi from Wuxi, Lu Xiaobo from Zhenjiang, Yu Xiaochuan, and leaders of chambers of commerce from major rice-producing areas such as Wujiang, Kunshan, Songjiang, Qingpu, and Rugao, should also join as initiators. Localities in counties with significant rice production could also follow suit and organize county associations. It is reported that the Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce received a letter yesterday from the Wuxi Chamber of Commerce, stating that the Jiangsu-Shanghai People's Food Regulation Association, initiated by Mu Ouchu, Jiang Wenyu, Wang Zhixin, Huang Renzhi, and others from the Shanghai Local Association, is scheduled to hold its establishment meeting at 4:00 PM on the 28th of this month at the Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce. They hoped to notify various counties and relevant organizations to attend. The Chamber has already notified various chambers of commerce and representatives of relevant organizations to attend the meeting in the province on time. (27th)

Recent Situation in Tibet 65

Tibet is located in the remote southwest frontier. Due to inconvenient transportation, the Chinese people know very little about its situation. We have gathered a relatively detailed report from various sources to share with the nation.

Politics: In Tibet, political power and religious authority have traditionally been separate and unrelated. In the 21st year of the Guangxu reign of the Qing Dynasty, the Dalai Lama, the religious king, imprisoned the political king, the Mo Buddha, and seized his seal of office. From then on, political and religious power were concentrated in the hands of the Dalai Lama. At that time, although the Qing government had troops stationed in Tibet, they were corrupt and incapable of fighting, and all Qing troops withdrew without a battle. After seizing both religious and political power, the Dalai Lama showed little regard for China. He acted unilaterally in foreign affairs and had to flatter the British due to geographical reasons. In recent years, the Dalai Lama, feeling his position was secure, gradually became less flattering to the British than before. Therefore, the current Dalai Lama is not as pro-British as he used to be, and the British are not as pro-Dalai Lama as they once were. However, a small group of subordinates still fawn over the British and collude with them. The Dalai Lama's political tactics are entirely about being smooth and adaptable, treating the British and the central government in the same way. On the one hand, he sends representatives to be permanently stationed in the central government, while on the other hand, he prepares for war and secretly buys weapons, constantly invading the border areas of Sichuan. He does this because the Dalai Lama knows that the central government has no time to care. The Dalai Lama's politics are entirely autocratic. Believers must regard him as sacred, and the people should view him as surpassing all emperors. His every word and action must be obeyed by the people. Therefore, the people have a situation of daring to be angry but not daring to speak out against him.

Economy: Due to repeated wars in recent years, the Tibetan economy has become increasingly depleted for both the government and the people. The Sichuan-Tibet war cost the people 3 million rupees. After the defeat in mid-May, more than 500,000 of military equipment was purchased from the British. As a result, merchants and ordinary people are facing a situation of sitting and waiting for death due to harsh taxes. Taking Lhasa as an example, more than fifty shops have closed down since February due to economic difficulties. The exhaustion of the Tibetan economy is due to the recent wars, but the long-term cause is the economic aggression of the British. When buying goods in Tibet, people must exchange Tibetan currency for rupees in India. In the past, four Tibetan silver dollars could be exchanged for one rupee, but now thirty Tibetan silver dollars are required to exchange for one rupee. In order to collect silver, the Dalai Lama manufactures copper coins, issues paper money, and forces the people to use them. Therefore, the people's assets are only in the form of copper and paper.

Military Affairs: The Tibetan army currently consists only of infantry. There are very few cavalry and artillery. The infantry is mostly drafted from the civilian population and receives very little training. Among them, there are more than five thousand well-trained infantry who have been trained by the British, Russians, and Japanese. This is the most elite part of the Tibetan army, currently stationed in the Longbulingka Garden. The military equipment is bought from India, which is equipment discarded by India. Recently, a batch of new-style rifles, machine guns, and mortars was purchased from the United Kingdom, which is a very unfavorable sign for the central government. The uniforms worn by the soldiers are all contracted by the British. Their style and color are exactly the same as those of British soldiers. The flag used by the army is a lion, with colors of red, yellow, blue, white, and black. The current army is about 50,000 people. Soldiers are between the ages of eighteen and sixty. Military pay includes 900 taels of barbarian silver per year for officers, and the Dalai Lama also grants land. If an officer dies in battle, the land granted after death is inherited by his children. Soldiers receive a monthly salary of four taels of silver, and the Dalai Lama also grants a certain amount of land. However, even if they die in battle, the land is not inherited by their descendants; instead, it is given to the soldier who fills the vacancy.

Society: Due to the cold weather in Tibet, there are very few products. Therefore, the living standards of the general population are extremely low. The main food of the people is barley, wheat, and green fruits. The upper class occasionally eats rice, but except for a small amount produced in Dui, most of it is purchased from India. Even daily necessities such as oil and salt are imported from India. Due to religious reasons, fish is prohibited from being cooked, so there are many fish in the ponds and lakes in Tibet. Marriage is dominated by polygamy. The scarcity of women and the hardship of life are the main reasons for implementing this system. Most lamas do not marry. The Dalai Lama himself has not married. All his associates are young lamas. It is rumored that there are secret women, but it is not dared to be made public for fear of losing the people's faith. Recently, the Dalai Lama has a confidant, who is also male, and has great influence in front of the Dalai Lama.

The People: The Tibetan people can be divided into three parts: one part is the people who support the Panchen Lama, one part is the people who support the Dalai Lama, and the other part is the Red and Yellow sects. The people who support the Panchen Lama often hope that the Panchen Lama will return to Tibet to get rid of the Dalai Lama's harsh rule. However, the Panchen Lama's return to Tibet is a difficult problem because his power is not equal to the Dalai Lama. Without a decisive method from the central government, there is no possibility of success.

In short, the instability in Tibet and the disputes in the southwest border of our country have no solution. Recently, the central government plans to change Tibet into a province. This is a good strategy for dealing with Tibet. Tibet is very poor in form, but in fact, its natural wealth is the best in the country. The reason why the British pay attention to Tibet is because they love its abundant mineral resources. The types of minerals include gold, silver, copper, iron, coal, etc., and the quality is good and the quantity is large. In a certain year, a Japanese person disguised himself as a Chinese person and sneaked into the mainland, spending several years of hard work to investigate minerals. The samples collected are worth more than one million yuan, which shows the abundance of mineral resources.

Anhui People Oppose Rice Tax 66

Bengbu Chamber of Commerce Sends Telegram to Yu Youquan to Block His Arrival

Bengbu Correspondence: The rice tax in Anhui Province is a disguised form of rice levy. When Chen Diaoyuan was the chairman of the Anhui Provincial Government, it was stopped due to repeated opposition from the people of Anhui and an order from the Executive Yuan, as well as an impeachment from the Supervisory Yuan. After the reorganization of the provincial government, the authorities, citing the emptiness of the provincial treasury and the exhaustion of finances, resumed collection in the name of managing food. First, rice and grain export inspection offices were set up in northern and southern Anhui, then changed to rice tax inspection offices, and later changed to rice and grain export administration bureaus. Now, Ye Yuanlong, the Director of the Department of Finance, has changed the method again and established the Anhui Provincial Food Export Management Committee in the provincial capital, formulating regulations, with Management Committee member Li Yunqi concurrently serving as the Director of the Wuhu Management Bureau, Lu Zhongnong concurrently serving as the Director of the Dashengguan Management Bureau, and Yu Youquan concurrently serving as the Director of the Bengbu Management Bureau. All three bureaus are under the jurisdiction of the Management Committee. The Bengbu Management Bureau also governs the Wangtai, Hao County, and Jieshouji sub-bureaus. After Yu Youquan was appointed, he departed from the province and will arrive in Bengbu in the coming days. The local Chamber of Commerce believes that the authorities are creating excuses to restore the rice tax, which is tantamount to collecting a disguised rice levy, and it is difficult to recognize. Yesterday, the chairman of the Chamber, Peng Zhuoru, sent a telegram to Yu Youquan, expressing his opposition. The original telegram stated: "To Mr. Yu Youquan of the Food Management Committee of the Anhui Provincial Government, Greetings. Recently, I read in the newspaper that you have been appointed as the Director of the Bengbu Rice Tax Bureau. As a fellow townsman, I offer my congratulations. However, in recent years, Anhui Province has been plagued by excessive taxes and levies. In addition, the rice tax is unbearable for the people of Anhui who have survived the disasters. At the National Food Conference, the central government issued an order to abolish the rice tax so that food can circulate throughout the country. Moreover, the rice tax has been repeatedly opposed by the local people. Your morality and reputation have long been admired by the local people. Even if the government believes that there is no source of funds for road construction, you should act in accordance with your original intention of loving your hometown and speak out for the people. If you do not do this, the people of Anhui will be disappointed, which is a pity for you. Zhuoru has known you for a long time and offers sincere advice. If there is anything inappropriate, please forgive me. Bengbu Chamber of Commerce, Peng Zhuoru, respectfully (25th)"

Local Correspondence

Songjiang 67

Election Dispute in Zhangjiabang Township: The township head of Zhangjiabang Township in the Ninth District was previously removed from office and ordered to be re-elected due to illegal elections. On the 22nd of this month, the re-election was held by District Chief Wang and supervisors at the home of Zhang Shunsuo in the township. Initially, the order was good. By 3:00 PM, the voting was completed and the ballots were about to be counted when Zhang Ziming, the nephew of Zhang Yonglin, the former director of the Xiaokunshan Township Administration Bureau, and Xia Fulan and Xia Fuzhang, the brothers and nephews of Township Head Xia Futang, started shouting and causing trouble because voters Yu Huilou and Ding Zixing did not vote for Xia Futang. Xia Futang seized the opportunity to call on the crowd to hold benches and wooden objects and throw them around, injuring many voters. The order was greatly disrupted. Later, the district chief and police officers suppressed and stopped the chaos. It was not until after 4:00 PM that the ballots were opened. As a result,

Zhu Zhiqing, Xia Futang, and others were elected. It is said that this re-election was to overturn the previous illegal election, so one party seemed to be organized and had a pre-determined plan to cause trouble and vent their anger. When the chaos occurred, voter Yu Huilou was seriously injured and is now being treated at Songjiang Hospital. Zhang Ziming and others have filed a lawsuit with the court.

Yesterday (27th) morning around 8:00, more than twenty bandit ships with more than a hundred bandits were discovered. Wuxi 70

The Lake Bandit Who Looted Ganlu Town Was Arrested: Shen Weikui, the head of the Second District of the Wuxi Water Police, ordered the various teams in his department to patrol the rivers daily to strengthen security, as theft cases in the four townships have occurred frequently recently. The sixth squad leader Wang Yunlong led the No. 1 patrol boat to inspect the Nan Shuangmiao area in the northern township the other day, and suddenly saw a person in the small tea shop in the town with a flustered look, which was very suspicious. Team leader Wang stepped forward to question him, but the person's speech was evasive. Team leader Wang knew that he was not a good person, so he immediately took him on the boat and sent him to the sixth team. Team leader Shi interrogated him severely. He confessed that his name was Yu Deyin, from Chaohu, 39 years old, and that on July 3, 1928, he looted the entire town of Ganlu and looted the guns of the second squad of the water police stationed in the town. Later, he went to Zhejiang to divide the spoils, and was chased by the Zhejiang water police chief Xu Pucheng, so they fled separately. I also fled to the countryside and was arrested. After the confession, Team leader Shi prepared a document and sent it to the district office for review.

The Tobacco and Alcohol License Tax Has Been Resolved: The tobacco and alcohol license tax in Jiangsu Province was initially due to the dispute between the ministry and the province, and later due to the problem of switching the tax tickets paid by tobacco and alcohol merchants when the province was in charge. After the ministry took over, the tax amount changed slightly, and most license merchants were waiting and watching. Chen Henian, the director of the local collection bureau, after taking over, due to the fact that the county's tax revenue was too far from the contract amount, repeatedly discussed solutions with the leaders of the tobacco and alcohol merchants. After two months, a solution was reached and collection began to be remitted to the provincial bureau. However, the amount of tax silver collected is not very large, so he still wants to find a way to rectify it.

Mr. Liu came to Zhenjiang on the 25th and gave a speech at the Chamber of Commerce at 2:00 PM on the 26th. He first stated the significance of the organization of the association, and then said that the civil wars in Lu and Chuan provinces must be stopped by the people with all their strength. To make foreign affairs and domestic political construction have a way, civil war must be abolished first, and reported on the work of the association, which is divided into three items: (1) Propaganda on the advantages and disadvantages of civil war and how to stop it (2) Mediation during the brewing and launching of civil war, (3) Adopting a policy of non-cooperation with those who are in civil war. The speech ended at 2:50 PM. Mr. Liu then took a car to Beijing to give a speech. After Mr. Liu's speech, Lu Xiaobo proposed to organize the Zhenjiang Branch of the Abolish Civil War Great Alliance, which was unanimously approved, and it was decided that today's meeting would be the first preparatory meeting, and the Zhenjiang members who participated in the Abolish Civil War Great Alliance would be the preparatory members, and the branch would be formally established before November 10.

Second One Branch Chat

Various Kinds of Fighting 93

— Zhan Lu

The "Shuo Wen Jie Zi" (an ancient Chinese dictionary) defines the character "鬥" (dòu, fight) as "two scholars facing each other, with weapons behind them, resembling the form of fighters." There are various kinds of "鬥" (dòu, fight). "鬥" (dòu) plus "市" (shì, market) becomes "鬧" (nào, noisy); "鬥" (dòu) plus "共" (gòng, together) becomes "鬨" (hòng, rowdy); "鬥" (dòu) plus "斷" (duàn, break) becomes "鬭" (dòu, struggle); "鬥" (dòu) plus "兒" (ér, child) becomes "閱" (yuè, review). I will now imitate Wang Anshi's (a famous reformer) style of creating new characters and compose the following new character explanations:

When important figures in the country fight over prestige and influence, the character "鬧" (nào, noisy) is appropriate. They make a big fuss for the sake of practical interests, focusing solely on profit and disregarding righteousness, displaying a strong mercenary spirit, hence the character "市" (shì, market) in the middle of "鬧" (nào).

When engaging in a decisive battle to suppress the communists, the character "鬨" (hòng, rowdy) is appropriate. The character "共" (gòng, together), representing the Communist Party, is in the middle of "鬨" (hòng). There is "鬨" (hòng) only when there are communists; without them, there would be no "鬨" (hòng).

Past private feuds in Guangdong province and current private feuds in Shandong province are appropriately described by the character "鬭" (dòu, struggle). "鬭" (dòu) has the same pronunciation as "鬥" (dòu), but with the addition of "斵" (zhuó, chop), it signifies the depletion of much vitality. For example, the Flying Eagle warship in the navy and the lives and property of the people of Yexian County have all been depleted under this character "鬭" (dòu).

The ongoing war in Sichuan between the two Lius is appropriately described by the character "閱" (yuè, review). The Book of Songs says, "Brothers quarrel within the walls." Although the two Lius are not brothers, they are uncle and nephew, so the war in Sichuan between the two Lius can only be described as the two Lius "reviewing" Sichuan. Moreover, the character "兒" (ér, child) in the middle of "閱" (yuè) clearly represents an ignorant child. In a time of national crisis, the uncle and nephew are still reviewing each other endlessly. If they are not ignorant children, then what are they?

If we want to defend against foreign aggression with one heart, we must have the Four No's Policy, which means no "鬧" (nào, noisy), no "鬭" (dòu, struggle), and no "閱" (yuè, review) domestically. 丨Note: Wang Anshi is the "Obstinate Prime Minister".

China Expert 94

— Jiang Ping

丨The French View of China丨

France is so far away from China, yet they shamelessly talk about the Three Principles of the People, and people in the Kuomintang inevitably make countless jokes. The French novelist Chautemps won the Grigo Prize for his book "On China," but the problem lies precisely in this book. Below are four minor mistakes cited to elicit laughter from the public.

He said: (Mr. Sun wrote his Three Principles of the People in Paris and later lost the original manuscript.) We all know that the Three Principles of the People were written by Mr. Sun in Shanghai and Guangzhou after the establishment of the Republic of China. The loss of his first draft was during the civil war in Guangzhou, when Mr. Sun's residence was burned down.

He said (Sun Ke is Jiang Jieshi's brother-in-law.) This conclusion is derived from the fact that Soong Ziwen is Jiang Jieshi's brother-in-law. Where does this kinship concept come from? He simply misunderstood the kinship between Jiang Jieshi and Sun Ke's stepmother.

He said: (Jiang Jieshi's aunt—Mrs. Soong Ziwen—once rescued Wu Tiecheng from prison.) We will not discuss whether Wu Tiecheng's release was due to Mrs. Soong's rescue, but according to friends familiar with current affairs,) when Wu Tiecheng was arrested, Jiang Jieshi had not yet married into the Soong family, and Mrs. Soong Ziwen was not yet engaged to him.)

He also said: (Soong Ziwen was so poor five years ago that he could not even afford a rickshaw, but now he bought the most beautiful Dahua Hotel in Shanghai for 15 million US dollars.)

In 1926, Soong Ziwen was already the Minister of Finance of the National Government. At that time, needless to say, he could afford rickshaws, even cars. Moreover, he never bought the Dahua Hotel. As far as we know, the owner of the Dahua Hotel is a banking group.

Chautemps is not to be blamed. He is just one of many people who hold erroneous views about China! Such errors are common among those who regularly read Western publications and are not surprising. In short, China is indeed too far away from them, too far away!

New York Nightlife 95

— Ms. Ye Hua

丨An Interesting Story About Wu Chaoshu丨

New York was originally named New Netherland. In 1664, the English seized it from the Dutch and gave it to the Duke of York, the brother of King Charles of England, and changed its name to the current name. In 1776, the United States became independent, and after years of development, its prosperity is comparable to that of Shanghai today. It has become the focus of world attention, and everyone wants to visit it. My friend Zhou Quan returned from the United States last month and talked about New York's nightlife. I will briefly describe a few things below;

The center of New York's nightlife is nightclubs. Nightclubs are divided into different levels, and people from small and weak nations are not allowed to enter the top nightclubs. Years ago, Ambassador to the United States Wu Chaoshu planned to visit a nightclub but was rejected over the phone. Later, the mayor of New York came forward to apologize and eventually set up a special seat to invite Wu to visit. Dancing in the nightclub has a unique style. After the dance, the dance partners freely sit down in pairs and talk about what they want to talk about, which is not as restrained between men and women as in Shanghai. Newnal is the most distinguished nightclub. The qualification to enter the nightclub is that one must have at least a million-dollar fortune. It is the patent of the so-called automobile kings, steel kings, etc. The furnishings inside are beyond imagination. The number of attendants is several times the number of tourists. It is located in front of Central Park and is adjacent to the residences of capitalists.

There are more than 60,000 female office workers in New York. Most of them are romantic. Every evening, they put on heavy makeup and gorgeous clothes, and stroll leisurely with young men. On the contrary, the waitresses in restaurants and bars are chaste and dutiful. The reason is not without economic background. The waitresses can earn a small income of 100 to 200 yuan in addition to their monthly salary of 40 to 50 yuan, which is enough to support themselves, while the female office workers only earn a meager salary per month, but they have high aspirations and extravagant habits, so they have to rely on others, adding a historical record to New York's nightlife.

Prostitution is not limited to our country; it is also prevalent in Europe and the United States. New York's prostitutes are not very different, but there is one thing worth mentioning: some brothels only provide housing facilities, which means they are "golden houses without beauties." Another type is the opposite, with beauties but no golden houses.

Opera is a gathering place for New York's nightlife, but the ticket prices are too high, often costing 70 to 80 yuan per person. The poor sigh in despair. Oil tycoon Rockefeller, thinking of the lower classes, donated 60 million US dollars to build a large theater that can accommodate 100,000 people. The ticket price is only 1 to 2 yuan. The theater occupies four blocks on 72nd Street in New York, which can be said to be huge. The engineers have carefully planned the sound and light distribution and the supply of cold and hot air, which is truly a masterpiece of world architecture. Alas! The reason why a civilized country is civilized is also due to human effort. May our countrymen not complain about heaven or blame others, but strive to improve themselves!

Roman Bullring, Painted by Liu Haisu 97

Liu Haisu's European Travel Works 98

— Shi Xun

In the last fifteen years, Liu Haisu has gained the highest authority in the Chinese art world and has had a great influence on recent painters. The ill-fated poet Xu Zhimo said;) ...From Haisu's works, we can see the trend of Haisu's life spirit. He is a man with physique and strength, and he can indeed restrain his innate physique and strength into his works. We cannot deny his broad mind, the development of his artistic conception, and the strength of his brushstrokes. You may not like his works, you may criticize his works from all aspects, but you cannot ignore his creation

the spirit and unique position, he is there, whether it is rough or fine, he is not only there, he also forces you to pay attention, making you unconsciously moved. ...) Xu Zhimo's words are correct, his lines have a unique talent, all his pictures are purely creative structures, and show his great, eternal and outstanding. Although he has been influenced by many masters, he has never lost himself, and his style has always been consistent. Each of his works is clearly showing us his temperament, his nature, the circumstances he encountered, the era he was born in, and the country he is in. That is the hope of boldness, strength, progress, and the new China in the East.

Now his representative work (Notre Dame de Paris at Sunset) is displayed at the exhibition, opposite the (Louvre); this is really the best proportion. The bronze-like color of the (Louvre) and the precise technique, (Notre Dame de Paris at Sunset) the fire-like sunshine and the wild charm, are very different in the eyes of ordinary people, but in fact they are one and two, and two and one, and at the same time can express his character and personality, and write out the secrets of nature.

People think that Liu is good at landscape, but they do not know that he is also good at human body and portrait. We see that most of the portraits he has produced this time, such as (Ma Xiangbo, Thinker) (Mrs. L), etc., a special majestic beauty makes people strange, his flying and vivid strokes can indeed express the deep sensuality and the spiritual joy and depression.

From his landscapes, we can see his depiction of the colors of various places, the brilliance of Venice, the strong colors of Rome, the beauty of the Swiss lakes and mountains, the sun and sunflowers of Belgium, the gray mystery and solemnity of Paris, all of which can give us infinite taste. As for the solidity of his buildings and the naive sense of the characters in the scene, they are all the gains he made after his European tour.

Postal Couple Entering the Pass (24) 99

— Seeking Happiness

Lu Boqin was also extremely moved, but there was still a bit of unresolved worry in his heart, and he murmured to Yi Dao;) For the fulfillment of love, we should both be happy. It's just that before entering Yu Pass, the road ahead is still full of thorns, and I don't know if we can escape from this tiger's mouth. If there is any mistake, my life is not worth regretting, but what if it involves you?)

(You are like this again!) Yi let go of her hand and broke away from the embrace, saying very calmly;) When I saw this passport, I regarded it as a formal marriage certificate, and I was very satisfied. Even if I have to go to die immediately, I will still think that my wish has been fulfilled, this life is not in vain, and I will die without regret!)

(Good! You have such great courage for love, why should I still be so cowardly? Let's hold hands and move forward boldly!) Lu Boqin also became excited and still dragged Yi into his arms with one hand. After being tender for a while, he whispered;) But be bold but careful. When we get on the train later, we must be careful.)

This is also where Lu Boqin is precocious and experienced; after he carefully told Tong Yizhen how to take a cautious and calm attitude, when they got on the train together that night, the two of them were calm and generous, very much like a married young couple, without revealing any flaws. Although they passed through several outposts and several teams of Japanese soldiers who were like wolves and tigers, they all passed safely.

After the train started, he and the other postal workers were all in a specially designated third-class carriage. Two Japanese soldiers, holding bayonet-mounted rifles, guarded the front and rear doors of the carriage, not allowing him to walk to other carriages. In addition, the lights in the carriage were also broken, and it was dark and gloomy like in a miserable hell, so they had to lean on each other on a wooden chair, and unknowingly fell asleep

Special Article 100

A Humble Proposal for Reforming Chinese School Education Thirteen Cheng Tianfang

It has been written in a rambling way, already more than ten thousand words, before the end of this article, there are still three issues to be discussed incidentally, the first is the atmosphere of learning, the second is physical education, and the third is military training, in the last ten years, the failure of the Chinese learning atmosphere is undeniable, some schools simply live in a storm all year round, not only the maintenance of discipline in the school, the training of group life, can not be talked about at all, even the minimum amount of homework that should be taught, is completely perfunctory, students mixed like this for six years in middle school, they become middle school graduates, mixed like this for four years in university, they become university graduates, the society is full of this kind of middle and university graduates, how can it not be bad, the country and society spend tens of millions of dollars every year to create this kind of people, it is really a heartbreaking thing, so if the learning atmosphere can not be reformed, any good education system can not produce good results, but how to reform it, in the past, the government mostly took a laissez-faire attitude towards student unrest, only in recent months has it strictly implemented sanctions, strict sanctions are naturally necessary, but I think that to reform the learning atmosphere, we must also rely on the efforts of the education community itself, in the past, some schools have experienced unrest, often because the principal and teachers have not been able to fulfill their responsibilities, and even want to use students to do their tools, since the principal and teachers can use students to attack others, students can naturally attack the principal and teachers in turn, so when a school experiences unrest, students are certainly wrong, the principal and teachers can not shirk responsibility, so to really rectify the learning atmosphere, the government's choice of principal, the principal's choice of teachers, must be particularly cautious, do not make people who fill the number, and at the same time the principal and teachers must also deeply understand their own responsibilities, be virtuous and disciplined, set an example, do not have the psychology of using young people, can get the faith of young people, guide young people to develop on the right track, most students in any school are always willing to be good, as long as the teachers and leaders are effective, the learning atmosphere can naturally be prosperous,

Local News

Unified Law Conference Interprets the Crime of Forging Graduation Certificates 104

Only When It Is Sufficient to Harm the Public or Others

Can a Criminal Charge Be Established

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau previously submitted a request to the Ministry of Education to clarify the penalties for forging academic or graduation certificates. The Executive Yuan consulted the judicial interpretation and resolved through the Unified Interpretation of Laws Conference that, in addition to forging official seals, which constitutes a crime under Article 235, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Code, the remaining forgeries of academic or graduation certificates and transcripts, etc., must be sufficient to harm the public or others to constitute a criminal charge. The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau further stated that the meaning of the phrase "must be sufficient to harm the public or others" seemed unclear and requested further clarification. The bureau argued that students who forge academic or graduation certificates to fraudulently obtain student status or positions often infringe upon the opportunities of others to study or serve due to quota limitations. The question was whether this situation should be considered harmful. The Unified Interpretation of Laws Conference resolved yesterday that student academic or graduation certificates or transcripts, etc., cannot be used to obtain student status or positions unless they have been reviewed and deemed authentic. Therefore, forging such documents is not inherently sufficient to cause harm to the public or others and does not constitute a crime. The resolution was sent to the Ministry of Education and forwarded to the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau for compliance. (New Voice Society)

Pan Gongzhan Does Not Advocate Taking Over Shanghai Middle School 105

Stating That It Is Better to Run Another School Than to Take It Over

Expresses That Selling Shanghai Middle School Is Feasible

丨Greatly Hopes That the French Concession Authorities Will Subsidize Private Education

(Central News Agency) Yesterday, a Central News Agency reporter specifically visited Pan Gongzhan, the Director of the Municipal Education Bureau, regarding the issue of the concession subsidizing private school funding and the transfer of Jiangsu Provincial Shanghai Middle School. He was kind enough to provide the following comments: (Question) It is rumored that the Provincial Shanghai Middle School will sell its original site. What are your opinions on this matter, Director? (Answer) I have also heard about this matter, but I believe that this matter is not impossible to handle. In the current situation, the sale of all the land of Shanghai Middle School can be worth at least five or six hundred thousand yuan. If we can purchase land and build school buildings in the remote areas of this city, then we can get several times larger than the original one. This is also an economical way. However, I believe that the selection of the new base of Shanghai Middle School should still be within the scope of this city. (Question) Regarding the transfer of Shanghai Middle School, during the time of former Director Xu, a request was submitted to the Municipal Government to ask the Central Government to strive for it. Are you still continuing that proposal? (Answer) I believe that there is no need to strive for this matter. It is not impossible for the Jiangsu Provincial Government to open a school within the scope of this city to supplement the lack of education in this city by contributing money. Moreover, the educational expenses of this city are currently in a difficult situation. In the future, if it is more abundant, it would be more beneficial to start a middle school separately than to take over Shanghai Middle School. Although I am a local official, I should still think about the entire country. (Question) The Shanghai Public Concession has already obtained the consent of the Public Concession authorities to subsidize the funding of private schools in the Concession. However, the French Concession levies heavier taxes on citizens than the Public Concession, and the educational undertakings run by Chinese people are less than the Public Concession. What opinions do you have on this matter, Director? (Answer) The reason why the Public Concession was able to propose a part of the funding to subsidize the private schools of the Chinese people in the past was actually due to the efforts of the Chinese Directors in the Concession. Therefore, I hope that the Chinese Directors in the French Concession can also base on this spirit and strive for it from the French Public Concession Bureau.

Physical Education

The First Day of the Citywide Elementary School Joint Sports Meet 107

Opening Ceremony Held Yesterday Morning 丨 50,000 Elementary School Students Attended as Spectators

105 Schools Participated 丨 Over 6,000 Athletes Performed and Competed

The long-awaited Shanghai Fourth Elementary School Joint Sports Meet opened at 9:00 AM yesterday. Over four hundred people attended the ceremony, including Bureau Chief of Land Affairs Jin Liren, representatives from the Municipal Education Association Tao Baichuan, representatives from the Private School Association Xu Zeyu, and representatives from various agencies. After the ceremony, Mayor Wu delivered the opening speech, Bureau Chief of Education Pan reported on the preparations, Municipal Party Representative Cai Hongtian gave an exhortation, and Bureau Chief of Health Li delivered a speech. The speeches were all cautionary and inspiring to the students. The Siemens company's loudspeakers broadcast the sound throughout the venue. After singing the sports meet anthem, the drill began, with Commander Chen Zize giving clear commands and Hu Zongfan demonstrating correct posture. Over two thousand elementary school students performed movements that were quite orderly and lively, which was no easy feat. After the drill, various sports events began.

丨A Glimpse of the Grand Scene丨

The venue's order was maintained by the East Asia Boy Scouts and the Shanghai South District Defense Corps. The music was performed by the Municipal Police Bureau band. The order was excellent, and the sound and color were magnificent, enhancing the spirit of the event. The venue's first aid was provided by the Bureau of Health.

Cheers reverberated around the venue, where the seats for various elementary schools were located, densely packed with no fewer than forty thousand people. Upon seeing their schoolmates win competitions, everyone cheered, demonstrating their keen interest.

Including the performing schools, a total of 105 schools participated (72 municipal and 33 private). The number of male and female track and field athletes reached over 1,800. The number of elementary school students participating in group exercises was even greater, reaching over 4,000. There were approximately 500 elementary school students attending as spectators. It can be said that this was an unprecedented grand event in the city.

Mayor Wu Delivers Opening Speech (Photo by Xu Tianzhang)

丨Details of the Opening Ceremony丨

The opening ceremony began at 9:00 AM yesterday morning. After the formal proceedings, Honorary Chairman Mayor Wu Tiecheng delivered a speech, followed by Chairman Bureau Chief Pan Gongzhan's report. Then, Municipal Party Representative Committee Member Cai Hongtian gave a speech, and finally, Li Ting'an delivered a speech. After the speeches, the participating students sang the sports meet anthem and performed the mass drill, which was extremely enthusiastic.

Chairman Mayor Wu's Exhortation: Officials of the Shanghai Elementary School Joint Sports Meet, elementary school students of Shanghai, we Chinese citizens must now save the nation. But what methods should we use? Are these methods effective? From our current perspective, saving the nation requires strengthening the race. If the race is strong, the nation will naturally be strong. Therefore, we pay attention to strengthening the race. This will not only save the nation but also make the country stronger day by day. Strengthening the race depends on education. The government and society must bear the responsibility of education and fulfill the way of education. If we bear the responsibility of education and fulfill the way of education, we will have good citizens. With good citizens, we will have a good government. With a good government, we can have good politics. With good politics, we can make the country stronger. Today's sports meet is the government fulfilling its responsibility of education, fulfilling the way of education, so that you elementary school students will all become sound citizens. You elementary school students must know the current danger of the nation and the difficulties our ancestors faced in founding the nation. Train your sound bodies to save the nation and preserve the land and all undertakings left to us by our ancestors.

Chairman Bureau Chief Pan's Report: This session of the Elementary School Joint Sports Meet is the fourth. It was originally scheduled to be held last autumn, but was temporarily suspended due to the Jingbei Incident. This time, in mid-September, we received approval from the municipal government and allocated funds to hold it. Preparations began on September 26th, establishing the rules and notifying the schools. The preparations have taken just over a month. This time, a total of 105 elementary schools are participating in the event, including 72 municipal schools and 33 private schools. There are 1,800 male and female track and field athletes, and over 4,000 participants in the group exercises. The event program, in addition to this morning's drill, includes male and female track and field events and group exercises. The group exercises are further divided into male and female rhythmic gymnastics, kindergarten student performances, and four types of national martial arts. The male and female track and field events are divided into four groups: A, B, C, and D, so that all elementary school students can participate. The event will last for three days, followed by a one-day public amateur sports meet on the 30th. The number of participants in this session is more than before and more enthusiastic than before, which shows that they have been stimulated by the national crisis and know that it is necessary to exercise. This time, we are very grateful for the awards given by all parties and for the help from the Public Security Bureau, the Public Utilities Bureau, and the Health Bureau.

Municipal Party Representative Cai Hongtian's Speech: Today is the Shanghai Elementary School Sports Meet. I am very honored to participate on behalf of the municipal party. We have two hopes for you today: (1) Sports competitions should only be a means, and the goal is exercise. Winning or losing is not important. Those who win should continue to work hard, and those who lose should not be discouraged but should work even harder. (2) The purpose of the sports meet is to exercise the body. You are participating to exercise, so I hope you will continue to exercise after the sports meet. Finally, I wish you all good health.

Bureau Chief of Health Li Ting'an's Speech: I am very honored to participate in this sports meet today. China is now in great danger. Saving the nation does not depend on money but on people, and on people's bodies. This sports meet is being held to promote physical education and to exercise your bodies. I hope you will work hard and each become a sound citizen to serve the nation in the future.

However, due to the unfavorable weather, it seems there may be two meanings. It is hereby pre-determined that if it is still raining at 8:00 AM on the 28th, the meeting will be suspended for the day, and the meeting will be postponed for one day. Datong Wins Basketball Charity Match Against Fudan 108

The Datong University basketball team, at the invitation of the Fudan University basketball team, held a charity match at the Fudan basketball gymnasium yesterday. At 7:30 PM, with Wu Shijie's whistle, the two sides began to compete. Datong took the lead and scored first. Fudan was unwilling to be outdone, taking advantage of opportunities to move, and with the different momentum of the home and away teams, the score increased frequently. In the first half, they took the lead with a score of 20 to 10. As the second half began, Datong changed its strategy and reorganized its lineup. Interception and throwing were both successful. As a result, the victory belonged to Datong with a score of 30 to 29.

Basketball New Techniques (20) (2) (Not Allowed) (Reprinted) Original work by Claire Burcky, translated and compiled by Zhang Guodong and Qian Yiqin

Can you recall Connie Mack and athlete Harvey Freeman? He invented a continuous rotation attack method to win the Michigan State C-level championship twice. The tactics are shown below.

Number one passes the ball to number two and immediately runs to the baseline. If he can escape the surveillance of the guard, number two can still pass the ball back to number one. However, under this circumstance, number one's guard will inevitably watch him extra closely. Then two people (number one and his guard) will just block number two's guard, giving number two a good opportunity to dribble forward and shoot. If number two is blocked by the opponent under the basket and cannot shoot, then he can pass to number four or number five who can get rid of his guard. This type of rotating attack uses the situation to control the ball and is consistent throughout, not stopping until the opponent's guard relaxes on his own. It is truly an attack that combines wisdom and courage.

Li Du Cables Repelling Advancing Japanese Troops 109

The Shanghai office of the Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang People's Support Association received a cable yesterday from the director of the headquarters, stating: We have received a cable from Li Du stating that since the first day of this month, over 700 Japanese troops and over 1,000 puppet Manchurian troops, via Jiamusi and Tulongshan, have advanced towards our defenses in Sandao Gang, Erdao Hezi, and Boli. Our troops, led by Chen Zongdai and a part of the 24th Brigade, met them head-on with a fierce attack. After seven days and nights of fierce fighting, our 26th Brigade reinforced them. The enemy's momentum could not withstand it, and they collapsed towards Yilan. Details will be reported separately. This is specially reported for your information.

退伍 Soldiers of the 61st Division Form Suicide Squad 110

Volunteering to go to Northeast China to Resist Japan and Save the Nation

According to the Huadong News Agency, Ouyang Zhiping and others, retired soldiers of the 61st Division of the 19th Route Army, have organized a suicide squad to resist Japan and save the nation and are about to depart. Yesterday, they issued a declaration stating: The violent Japanese, with their East Asian continental policy, use their sharp cannons as a vanguard. Last year, on September 18th, they captured Liaoning and Jilin. This spring, on January 28th, they attacked our Songhu. Although our army met them head-on in the Battle of Songhu, inflicting heavy losses on the enemy, the enemy had no choice but to comply with the agreement and endure their loss of troops and retreat north. However, the powerful neighboring Japanese, not only did not repent of their evil deeds but also became even more intensified. Now, they have moved the troops from Songhu, devoting all their strength to threatening our Northeast volunteer army as much as possible, intending to support puppets to achieve their final goal of the Manchurian policy. At the same time, they are attacking Rehe and harassing the security of Pingjin to disrupt world public opinion. Our government's countermeasures, at this time when volunteer armies are arising one after another, the war clouds are densely covering Rehe, and the momentum is urgent. We have witnessed enemy planes in Songhu, suffered from the bombing of huge bombs, and heard the sounds of fierce cannons and loud shouts of killing. We have long understood the enemy's magic weapons and the abilities of their soldiers. How can we allow them to hide their flags and silence their drums here, silently sucking our blood? How can we sit idly by and watch Rehe become the second Shenyang, allowing it to fall? And the cries of suffering from our Northeast compatriots, and the weeping and wailing sounds of the anti-Japanese martyrs, how can we turn a deaf ear? Otherwise, if our Chinese nation wants to seek its survival, recover lost territory, and avenge its humiliation, it can only fight desperately, strive to the death, and resist to the end. The Northeast volunteer army is looking forward to increasing the front line, adding infantry, and preparing for a counterattack. The Rehe side is especially awaiting assistance to make a fierce resistance. Under these circumstances, we anti-Japanese soldiers have only our bodies and lives. We must intensify the anti-Japanese movement, and continue to fight a life-and-death battle with the enemy. Now, we and our comrades vow to use our blood and heads to resolve to go north to aid Rehe, or to leave the pass and work together with the Northeast volunteer army to resist Japan and save the nation. We will fight together for our national mission. This is our solemn declaration.

Mr. Yan Ziduan's Talk on Developing the Northwest 112

The first batch of members of the Northwest Reclamation Corps returned to Shanghai a few days ago. Details have already been recorded in this newspaper. However, the head of the corps, Mr. Yan Ziduan, delayed his return to Shanghai until yesterday because he still needed to liaise with various sectors along the way. According to Mr. Yan, he led twenty corps members from Shanghai on August 1st. They traveled via the capital to the Jinpu Railway to Jinan, then through Tianjin to Beijing. After staying in Beijing for several days, they transferred to the Pingsui Railway, passing through Suiyuan and other places, and arrived at their destination, Baotou. They then set up an office on Qianmen Street in Baotou to facilitate communication with the headquarters in Shanghai. They spent over forty days in Baotou investigating reclamation. Because there were matters to attend to in Shanghai, he sent a standing team to Baotou and led a small number of comrades back to Shanghai. He plans to make a second expedition next spring. The land in Suiyuan is particularly fertile, especially the Hetao area. Hetao includes the three counties of Wuyuan, Linhe, and Dayutai, with Wuyuan as the center. Wuyuan straddles the Yellow River, divided into two parts, one outside the loop and one inside the loop. The total area of the county is 388,000 square miles. The terrain is flat, and most of it is suitable for farming, with the Hetao area being the most fertile. The main products are fur and livestock. Guihua and Baotou are the central locations for exporting these goods. More than ten foreign companies have established shops there to purchase wool, cashmere, cowhides, and horse hides. It is estimated that Guihua exports over 7 million pieces of leather, over 8 million catties of wool and cashmere, and 60,000 to 70,000 heads of livestock each year. The number of exports from Baotou is even greater. In addition, mineral resources are abundant, with salt ponds and coal as the main commodities. Salt ponds are mostly located in the Ordos region, and coal is distributed in the Daqingshan Mountains. According to geological surveys, there are reserves of 650 million tons of anthracite coal and 1.3 billion tons of bituminous coal. The richness of the geology is evident. Other aspects are too numerous to be described at one time. In short, developing the Northwest is the most important task of the day. In recent years, internal wars have continued, and disasters have been frequent. In addition, the violent Japanese have looted the Northeast. The people in the war zones and disaster areas who have been ruined are unprecedented in nearly sixty years. The old fill the gullies, and the young become bandits, forming a chaotic situation in China. If the Northwest can be reclaimed, it would be a good way to settle refugees from the disaster areas.

Beixin Bookstore Vandalized Yesterday 113

Losses Estimated at Over a Thousand Yuan

The Bookstore Temporarily Suspended Operations

According to a Central News Agency report, around noon yesterday, the distribution office of the Beixin Bookstore on Fuzhou Road was suddenly vandalized by a group of over thirty people speaking with Northern accents, causing losses of over a thousand yuan. The details are as follows:

Details of the Vandalism: At the time, about thirty people arrived at the bookstore, some in cars and some in rickshaws. After gathering at the entrance, more than ten people remained guarding outside the shop, while more than ten people rushed into the shop and asked if they had "Little Pigsy" for sale. The store had previously stopped selling the book after it caused offense to Muslims, who had negotiated with the bookstore. When someone asked to buy it, Zhao Shiyuan, the acting director of the bookstore's retail department, politely replied that the book was no longer for sale and that all remaining copies had been stored away. The group then asked to see the manager. Zhao replied that the manager was out. A verbal conflict ensued, and order was lost. The six bookstore employees were having lunch at a table. The group overturned the table, shattering bowls and dishes on the floor. The employees fled in different directions. The group then pulled out iron bars and smashed all the glass in the bookshelves. Those guarding outside the store simultaneously smashed all three large pieces of glass in the outer display windows. Zhao Shiyuan, the acting director of the bookstore, in desperation, ran out of the store and blew a police whistle borrowed from a nearby shop. Upon hearing the sound, the group jumped into cars and rickshaws and fled. By the time the police arrived, no one was left. The bookstore then closed its iron gates and temporarily suspended operations.

Muslims Express Their Views: After the incident, a reporter from the New Voice News Agency visited several Muslim leaders and officials of the Muslim Association, including Ma Xingzhong. According to Mr. Ma, he did not know that the Beixin Bookstore had been vandalized, and he did not believe that Muslims were responsible. He said that Muslims were well-organized and extremely obedient to the orders of their leaders. He added that Muslims had repeatedly held meetings to discuss the offensive text published by the Beixin Bookstore and had already decided to retain lawyer Wu Kaisheng to negotiate according to the law and would never take any further drastic actions.

Statement from the Bookstore: Zhao Shiyuan, the acting director of the Beixin Bookstore's retail department, told a reporter from the Central News Agency that the bookstore had received a letter of negotiation from lawyer Wu Kaisheng on behalf of the mosques three days ago and had stored away the book and stopped selling it, willing to await a legal solution. At the same time, the bookstore's wholesale department on Qipu Road also received a warning letter asking the bookstore and its manager to be careful. The bookstore reported the letter to the Shanghai Municipal Council Police Station for filing. Unexpectedly, the next day (i.e., the day before yesterday), at around 7:00 PM, a brick tied with grass rope was thrown into the retail department, breaking the glass window in the center. Today (i.e., yesterday), it was vandalized again, which was very unfortunate. The display windows are completely destroyed, and it will not be possible to resume business for several days. The damaged glass and musical instruments consigned by the Datong Music Society are worth over a thousand yuan. Police officers have come to investigate and have taken away an iron bar left behind by the group. Police officers are also protecting the wholesale department on Qipu Road.

According to the New Voice News Agency's investigation yesterday, the incident was believed to have been triggered by the bookstore's publication of the book "Little Pigsy." When the bookstore published the book, it was entirely based on descriptions in "Journey to the West" with added embellishments. It did not initially consider offending Muslims and therefore sold the book. A week ago, the bookstore received a letter from Muslims, and someone came to the bookstore requesting that the book be removed from sale and destroyed. The wholesale department on Qipu Road then retrieved the book and stopped selling it. However, the request for a public apology was not fulfilled.

Details of the Negotiations: The Muslim mosques in Fuyou Road, Nanmen, Rihuigang, Xieqiao, Xiaotaoyuan, Pudong, Xiaoshadu, Taopeng Road, Zhejiang Road, and Gordon Road, all believed that the book "Little Pigsy" was offensive to Islam. They jointly retained lawyer Wu Kaisheng to negotiate with the Beixin Bookstore. After accepting the case, lawyer Wu sent a letter to the Beixin Bookstore the day before yesterday to initiate negotiations. After receiving the letter, the bookstore appointed lawyer Wei Wenhan to go to the joint office of the Muslim mosques yesterday to discuss a settlement, but without success. At the same time, the joint office of the Muslim mosques dispatched representatives to the municipal government around 3:00 PM yesterday to petition for strict handling of the matter and planned to go to Nanjing within days to petition the central government.

Text of the Petition: Da Pusheng, the Imam of the Fuyou Road Mosque in Shanghai, and others, separately presented petitions to the National Government, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Interior, and various ministries, requesting punishment for the Beixin Bookstore. The original text reads: (Titles omitted) "In recent years, our country has been plagued by internal strife and increasing foreign aggression. The people are in turmoil, and the nation is in a precarious state. At this critical moment of survival, we must rely on the harmony of the people and promote unity to consolidate the spirit of all five ethnic groups and suppress internal and external threats so that the country can achieve peace. Unexpectedly, the Beixin Bookstore in Shanghai recently published a book called 'Little Pigsy,' which claims that Pigsy is the ancestor of Muslims and that Muslims are Little Pigsy. The book contains arbitrary insults and obscene content. The cover of the book features an ugly image of Pigsy printed in red to attract attention. Upon reading the book, Muslims in Shanghai were shocked. They believe that the bookstore deliberately intends to provoke the 50 million Muslims in the country, to instigate ethnic hatred between the Han and Hui people, and to create turmoil in the Northwest, so that the country cannot attend to internal affairs and achieve its goal of division and discord. Its malicious intention is truly profound and concerning for the future of China. The Muslims have no dealings with this bookstore. Why must it publish such a red book, defaming Muslims so severely? What is the intention behind inciting the Muslim community? We Muslims deeply understand the greater picture. We lodged complaints with the mosques in Shanghai. Although they harbor righteous indignation, they are all willing to obey the orders of the imams and seek redress from your Excellencies through proper channels. Representatives of the mosques have been meeting and discussing for days, carefully considering the matter. They believe that the bookstore's publication is an insult to individual Muslims, which can be addressed by ordinary laws. However, the insult is to Muslims both in China and abroad. There are no fewer than 50 million Muslims in China, and countless others who believe in Islam in other countries. Can they all endure this silently? It will inevitably lead to conflicts between the two religions, as in India and the provinces of Xinjiang. Even within Shanghai alone, there are no fewer than 100,000 Muslims. What method can be used to suppress their resentment? China is now in an extremely weak state, relying entirely on the unity of the five ethnic groups since the beginning of the revolution to consolidate the nation. Unfortunately, there are already groups among the ethnic groups that are splitting apart. The Muslim community wholeheartedly aims to save the world, and the patriotic armies mostly consist of courageous men. If the bookstore so offends the Muslim community, what if the entire community is disheartened and, after deep consideration, turns against the nation and neglects its defenses? The great disaster of a wildfire starting from a small spark will be this book's legacy. This is what we feel is dangerous, and we dare not refrain from speaking our minds earnestly. The original book has been submitted to the Shanghai Municipal Government for review. We respectfully submit this petition, imploring your Excellencies to telegraph the Shanghai Municipal Government to investigate the case and to investigate whether the bookstore has committed any crimes against national security in its previous publications to prove its intention to incite the Muslim community this time. As for this book, which endangers the public, the case is serious. What kind of national law should be applied is not something that the mosques dare to presume. The mosques have always maintained peace and followed the teachings of the scriptures, always remaining calm. Therefore, we endure humiliation and submit these humble words. How to appease the anger of the Muslims and how to alleviate the worries of the country is something that your Excellencies understand as clearly as the blue sky, and it does not require the mosques or the Muslims to make any requests. Furthermore, the editors of the book are Lin Lan, Zhu Yangshan, and the distributors are Li Zhiyun and Li Xiaofeng, all of whom are listed in the book. We submit this petition with grief and imploring sincerity." Imams Da Pusheng of the Fuyou Road Mosque in Shanghai, Ha Decheng of the Zhejiang Road Foreign Mosque, Ma Jingwu of the Xiaotaoyuan Mosque, and others respectfully kowtow. Temporary Office: Zhejiang Road Mosque.

Czech Nationals Celebrate Independence Day Today 116

Today is the 14th anniversary of Czechoslovakia's declaration of independence. The Czech Consul General in Shanghai, Mr. Le Faer, will lead the Czech nationals in a grand celebration. The Slavs established their country on this land as early as the 7th century, and the Kingdom of Bohemia in the Czech Republic was also very prosperous in the 14th century. In the 16th century, the Habsburg Dynasty also became the Kingdom of Bohemia, and then merged with Austria to form the United Kingdom. Later, due to the discrimination and abuse of the Austrian King, the Czechs and Slavs revived the idea of ​​national restoration. At the beginning of the nineteenth century, there was a movement for national restoration. When the European War broke out, the Czechoslovak National Committee was established in Paris. The current President Masaryk and Foreign Minister Beneš were both key figures in the committee at that time. They immediately recruited Czech nationals and formed an army to assist the Allied countries in France, Russia, and Italy, with outstanding achievements. In June 1918, the National Committee was recognized internationally as the future government of Czechoslovakia, and the Czechoslovak army was also recognized as the official Allied army participating in the war. On October 14 of the same year, the Czechoslovak Declaration of Independence was signed in Paris, and four days later, the Czechoslovak Declaration of Independence was issued by Masaryk. Ten days later, the Declaration of Independence was issued in Prague. The Provisional Government moved back to the country, opened a parliament, drafted a constitution, and elected Masaryk as president. Although the country has not been established for a long time, the people are united, the foundation of the country is solid, and industry and commerce are thriving, full of the vitality of a new country, and the future is promising.

Reforming Customs Administration Issues 117

Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Representatives Petition with Satisfaction

According to a New Voice News Agency report from Nanjing on the 27th, the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce believes that under the current customs administration, the customs commissioner can impose heavy fines with unilateral command. Since there is no grace period for execution and no remedy for appeals, it has dispatched representatives Lu Wenshao, Jin Runxiang, Tu Kaizheng, Zheng Zenan, Zhuang Honggao, Shi Zongtang, and Xie Zhongle to Nanjing on the morning of the 12th to petition the Central Party Headquarters, the Executive Yuan, the Legislative Yuan, the Ministry of Finance, and the Ministry of Industry. It requested that customs laws be formulated as soon as possible, and that detailed regulations be made on the procedures for penalties for tax evasion, remedies for dissatisfaction with rulings, and restrictions on the use of fines. It is heard that the central government appreciated the requests of the petition representatives and agreed that the responsible departments would start planning immediately. The petition representatives also petitioned the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Finance to strictly define the scope of customs anti-smuggling measures and to effectively stop recent bizarre actions. The ministries all agreed to investigate thoroughly to ensure that the people are not disturbed and that business development is not hindered. The representatives considered this satisfactory.

Statements from Responsible Personnel at the Jianghai Customs

According to a Central News Agency report, more than 100 trade associations in Shanghai expressed resentment over the Jianghai Customs' search for tax-evading goods, including searching shops, moving goods, and arbitrarily imposing fines. They sent a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to convene a general meeting to make a decision and dispatch representatives to Nanjing the day before yesterday to request reform of customs administration. A reporter from the Central News Agency visited the responsible personnel at the Jianghai Customs yesterday to inquire about the above-mentioned issues. According to them, searching for tax evasion is the responsibility of customs officials. Merchants should pay taxes in accordance with the tax regulations. Those who seek petty profits, violate the regulations, and smuggle and evade taxes have been repeatedly investigated and punished. There are also many who have not been caught smuggling. The customs authorities have to carry out strict searches in order to rectify the national treasury revenue. As for entering shops to search, they will of course obtain considerable evidence and notify the court of the district in advance. The court will transfer a document to the police station, and customs officers will go to search together. This is an extremely legitimate method and the necessary procedure for customs officers to search for tax-evading goods. They hope that merchants will understand this point and hope that they will pay taxes in accordance with the tax regulations. As for reforming customs administration, this is another issue. If the public believes that the current customs administration needs to be reformed, they should petition the National Government for reform. The reporter also asked that if a merchant is found to have evaded taxes and believes that the customs' penalty is too heavy and disagrees with the ruling, what remedies are available? According to the reply, remedies for disagreeing with the customs' ruling is also one of the reasons why Shanghai merchants are requesting reform of customs administration. According to regulations, if the customs finds tax-evading goods, it will impose a fine of several times the value of the goods. As a result, merchants deliberately reduce the value of the seized goods in order to reduce the fine. The so-called disagreement with the ruling is this point. Attempting to reduce the fine is human nature. However, customs has a lot of experience in assessing the value of goods. As for the restrictions on penalties for tax evasion, etc., customs already has clear regulations.

According to the Central News Agency, National Government Chairman Lin Zichao suffered from asthma before and has not fully recovered. Yesterday, he again consulted with national doctor Lu Zhong'an for treatment. According to Chairman Lin's staff, Chairman Lin will return to Nanjing today or tomorrow. The Implementation Plan for Relieving Unemployed Workers was Discussed and Agreed Upon Yesterday 121

Individuals Were Assigned to Draft Separately

A Deadline Was Set for Submission and Reorganization

The Shanghai Municipal Government's plan to relieve unemployed workers, after being drafted by the Social Affairs Bureau and approved and supplemented item by item by the Municipal Government, held its first meeting yesterday. Details are as follows:

Meeting Details: The first meeting of the drafting committee for the implementation plan of the unemployed worker relief plan was held in the auditorium of the Social Affairs Bureau yesterday morning at 10:00 AM. Committee members Zhang Zhenyuan, Wang Keqing, Tian Heqing, Wang Gang, Cai Zhengya, Tai Hongji, Qian Zhongnan, Chen Lengseng, Shao Tongxuan, Rao Qiangsheng, and Hang Ding'an attended. Cai Zhengya chaired the meeting, and Jiang Shifu recorded. The chairman first reported on the process of being ordered to draft the implementation plan, and then the discussion began. The meeting adjourned at 12:00 PM.

Page 14

Various Plans: The various plans approved and supplemented by the Municipal Government are as follows: (A) Benefiting Labor: (1) Establish a municipal job placement center; (2) Establish a small handicraft loan office; (3) Raise a fund for unemployed relief; (4) Urge factories to establish worker savings associations; (5) Urge trade unions to establish consumer cooperatives; (6) Urge factories to establish labor schools or labor classes; (7) Urge factories to organize other activities to benefit labor; (B) Developing Industry: (1) Urge factories to improve products; (2) Encourage cost reduction; (3) Improve marketing methods; (4) Establish a municipal model factory; (C) Eliminating Labor Disputes: (1) Urge factories to organize factory conferences; (2) Improve the handling of labor disputes; (3) Prevent the instigation of labor strikes; (4) Stipulate standards for reducing business scope and closing down; (5) Stipulate minimum wage rates; (D) Developing the Rural Economy: (1) Improve agricultural affairs; (2) Urge the establishment of rural cooperatives; (3) Establish warehouses for storing agricultural products; (4) Award auxiliary methods; (5) Adjust the supply and prices of agricultural products;

Matters Resolved: A chief editor was appointed, with Cai Zhengya and Zhang Zhenyuan taking on the role. (1) How should the various relief plans be implemented separately? It was resolved to assign Wang Gang, Chen Lengseng, Zhang Zhenyuan, Hang Ding'an, Tian Heqing, Qin Hongji, Shen Xiongqing, Chen Zeyi, Cai Zhengya, and Qian Zhongnan to separately sue for the implementation of various plans. (2) Should a member be designated for each section to take on a dedicated role? It was resolved that Qin Hongji would be in charge of the second section, Wang Gang would be in charge of the third section, and Chen Lengseng would be in charge of the fourth section. (4) How should a deadline be set for drafting the implementation plan? It was resolved that the deadline should be before November 10, and it was stipulated that it should be completed within one week after submission.

Methods of the China Merchants Yarn and Cloth Exchange Responding to the Monthly Donation Campaign 123

Monthly Donation of 2,900 Yuan

Since the Northeast Refugee Relief Association launched the monthly donation campaign and announced its declaration, all sectors have responded and competed to be the first. Yesterday, the association received a letter from the China Merchants Yarn and Cloth Exchange, stipulating seven monthly donation methods: (1) Employees with salaries of 25 yuan or less can donate or not as they wish; (2) Those with 26 yuan to 50 yuan donate 1% of their monthly salary; (3) Those with 50 yuan to 75 yuan donate 2% of their monthly salary; (4) Those with 75 yuan to 100 yuan donate 3% of their monthly salary; (5) Those with 100 yuan or more donate 5% of their monthly salary; (6) The exchange doubles the total amount donated by employees; (7) The 70 brokers in the exchange assume that each donates 30 yuan. According to this method, employees can donate 400 yuan per month, and the exchange donates the same amount. Assuming that brokers donate 2,100 yuan, the total monthly donation is 2,900 yuan. Once a certain amount has been collected, it will be remitted to the bank on a monthly basis. This method of the exchange is thorough and fair. Not only is it enthusiastic about relief and advocates for all sectors, but it can also be imitated by companies and institutions.

Special District Office for Rickshaw Industry Approves Aviation Monthly Donation Method 126

Brigadier General Weng Zhaoyuan, the national hero who bravely defended Wusong with the 19th Route Army, will soon represent the China Aviation Construction Association to negotiate with overseas Chinese communities for the construction of China's aviation program to strengthen national defense and alleviate national crisis. However, the organization and equipment within the country require significant funding. He recently sent a letter to the Special District Office for the Rickshaw Industry seeking assistance. Upon receiving the letter, which coincided with the autumn members' general meeting and dinner at the Xiangbin Restaurant on Guangxi Road, the temporary chairman, Mr. Liang Ruiting, submitted it to all attending members for their support. Committee members including Director Gu Songmao, Yin Zhiling, Zhu Hebi, Xia Muyao, and Hou Shaoan successively voiced their opinions, all agreeing that the nation was facing a crisis and aviation equipment was extremely urgent. They recalled that the Battle of Zhabei was lost due to the lack of air force. If the country falls, the homes will be destroyed, and how can our rickshaw industry survive alone? They called for raising funds for aviation construction to equip the air force specifically for resisting foreign aggression and not for internal strife, stating that it was the duty of citizens. All rickshaw operators also publicly elected Yin, Gu, Zhu, Xia, and Hou as representatives for the meeting. As a result, they voluntarily agreed to donate to aviation construction for six months. In the first month, each rickshaw would donate one yuan, and in the second to sixth months, each rickshaw would donate half a yuan per month. The donations would be collected simultaneously with the November donation payment. Cai Qingtao, Yin Zhiling, Hou Shaoan, Xia Muyao, and Zhu Hebi were publicly elected as custodian committee members, responsible for safekeeping and depositing the funds in banks, converting them into whole sums, and notifying the Aviation Construction Association for disbursement and equipment, serving as aviation construction funds. A letter has already been sent to the association for verification. It is expected that all industry associations in Shanghai are enthusiastic and patriotic, and will definitely not be stingy, watching the country and homes fall, while the Special District Office for the Rickshaw Industry continues to exist.
